           <p>
            What files should be in my
            <code>
             .gitignore
            </code>

        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="17803964" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1410" id="answer-17803964" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="17803964">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1410" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1410
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/17803964/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Updated to Android Studio 3.0
             </strong>
             Please share missing items in comments.
            </p>
            <p>
             A late answer but
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/16640566/which-files-shouldnt-be-checked-in-into-version-control-in-android-studio">
              this
             </a>
             alternative answer was not right for us ...
            </p>
            <p>
             So, here's our gitignore file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>#built application files
*.apk
*.ap_
*.aab
                           
# files for the dex VM
*.dex
                            
# Java class files
*.class
                            
# generated files
bin/
gen/
                            
# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties
                        
# Windows thumbnail db
Thumbs.db
                
# OSX files
.DS_Store
                            
# Android Studio
*.iml
.idea
#.idea/workspace.xml - remove # and delete .idea if it better suit your needs.
.gradle
build/
.navigation
captures/
output.json 
    
#NDK
obj/
.externalNativeBuild
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Since Android Studio 2.2 and up to 3.0, new projects are created with this gitignore file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>*.iml
.gradle
/local.properties
/.idea/workspace.xml
/.idea/libraries
.DS_Store
/build
/captures
.externalNativeBuild
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Deprecated
             </strong>
             - for older project format, add this section to your gitignore file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>
/*/out
/*/*/build
/*/*/production
*.iws
*.ipr
*~
*.swp
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This file should be located in the project's root folder and not inside the project's module folder.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Edit Notes:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Since version 0.3+ it seems you can commit and push *
               <strong>
                .iml
               </strong>
               and
               <strong>
                build.gradle
               </strong>
               files. If your project is based on Gradle: in the new open/import dialog, you should check the
               <code>
                "use auto import"
               </code>
               checkbox and mark the
               <code>
                "use default gradle wrapper (recommended)"
               </code>
               radio button. All paths are now relative as @George suggested.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Updated answer according to @128KB
               <a href="https://github.com/google/iosched/blob/master/.gitignore" rel="noreferrer">
                attached source
               </a>
               and @Skela suggestions
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Building on my normal Android
             <em>
              .gitignore
             </em>
             , and after reading through documentation on the Intellij IDEA website and reading posts on StackOverflow, I have constructed the following file:
            </p>
            <pre><code># built application files
*.apk
*.ap_

# files for the dex VM
*.dex

# Java class files
*.class

# built native files (uncomment if you build your own)
# *.o
# *.so

# generated files
bin/
gen/

# Ignore gradle files
.gradle/
build/

# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties

# Proguard folder generated by Eclipse
proguard/

# Eclipse Metadata
.metadata/

# Mac OS X clutter
*.DS_Store

# Windows clutter
Thumbs.db

# Intellij IDEA (see https://intellij-support.jetbrains.com/entries/23393067)
.idea/workspace.xml
.idea/tasks.xml
.idea/datasources.xml
.idea/dataSources.ids
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Also note that as pointed out, the
             <em>
              built native files
             </em>
             section is primarily useful when you are building your own native code with the Android NDK. If, on the other hand, you are using a third party library that includes these files, you may wish to remove these lines (*.o and *.so) from your .gitignore.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="18454251">

            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="83" itemprop="upvoteCount">

            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Updated 7/2015:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Here is the
             <a href="https://intellij-support.jetbrains.com/entries/23393067">
              definitive source from JetBrains
             </a>
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <h2>
             Directory based project format (.idea directory)
            </h2>
            <p>
             This format is used by all the recent IDE versions by default. Here is what you need to share:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              All the files under
              <code>
               .idea
              </code>
              directory in the project root
              <strong>
               except
              </strong>
              the
              <code>
               workspace.xml
              </code>
              and
              <code>
               tasks.xml
              </code>
              files which store user specific settings
             </li>
             <li>
              All the
              <code>
               .iml
              </code>
              module files that can be located in different module directories (applies to IntelliJ IDEA)
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Be careful
             </strong>
             about sharing the following:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Android artifacts that produce a signed build (will contain keystore passwords)
             </li>
             <li>
              In IDEA 13 and earlier
              <code>
               dataSources.ids
              </code>
              ,
              <code>
               datasources.xml
              </code>
              can contain database passwords. IDEA 14
              <a href="https://youtrack.jetbrains.com/issue/IDEA-127105#comment=27-765064">
               solves this problem
              </a>
              .
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             You may consider not to share the following:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              gradle.xml file, see
              <a href="https://youtrack.jetbrains.com/oauth?state=%2Fissue%2FIDEA-55923">
               this discussion
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              user dictionaries folder (to avoid conflicts if other developer has the same name)
             </li>
             <li>
              XML files under
              <code>
               .idea/libraries
              </code>
              in case they are
              <strong>
               generated from Gradle
              </strong>
              project
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             Legacy project format (
             <code>
              .ipr
             </code>
             /
             <code>
              .iml
             </code>
             /
             <code>
              .iws
             </code>
             files)
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Share the project
              <code>
               .ipr
              </code>
              file and all the
              <code>
               .iml
              </code>
              module files,
              <strong>
               don't share
              </strong>
              the
              <code>
               .iws
              </code>
              file as it stores user specific settings
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             While these instructions are for IntelliJ IDEA, they hold true 100% for Android Studio.
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             Here is a
             <code>
              .gitignore
             </code>
             snippet that incorporates all of the above rules:
            </p>
            <pre><code># Android Studio / IntelliJ IDEA 
*.iws
.idea/libraries
.idea/tasks.xml
.idea/vcs.xml
.idea/workspace.xml
</code></pre>
           </div>

                 Which SDKs are supported is defined in the AndroidManifest.xml (and also by Gradle). Any SDK allowed by that setting must be ok for development. Concerning code styles: this is not something that has to be maintained in each project separately, and moreover it should be clarified independent of the IDE. Copyright headers: hopefully, these are in your code base and not in any IDE project files. Otherwise building on the commandline would simply not include them...
                </span>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @Risadinha 1) SDKs are defined at the IDE level as well. They are referenced in the Manifest, but the project file contains the actual SDK definitions. 2) Code style should be maintained AT LEAST at the project level. Ideally, everyone would write standard Java, but oh well. 3) Copyright headers are stored in the project. They are used for new file creation, and can contain macros for name, company name, project, date, etc. I recommend you check them out!  In summary, the project files contain important meta information about the project that needs to be shared and controlled across the team.
                </span>

                 JetBrains has deprecated DOC-1186 and put their
                 <a href="https://intellij-support.jetbrains.com/entries/23393067" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  updated recommendations in a new post
                 </a>
                 : DO INCLUDE: All the files under .idea directory in the project root except the workspace.xml and tasks.xml, and all the .iml files. BE CAREFUL when sharing Android artifacts that produce a signed build (will contain keystore passwords), dataSources.ids and datasources.xml (they may contain passwords). CONSIDER EXCLUDING: gradle.xml, user dictionaries folder, and XML files under .idea/libraries (in case they are generated from Gradle project).

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="24679853" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="4" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="47" id="answer-24679853" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="24679853">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             </svg>

              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I disagree with all of these answers.  The following configuration is working great for our organization's app.
            </p>
            <p>
             I ignore:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               /build
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               /.idea
              </code>
              (with possible exceptions, see comments in
              <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/23504260/1747491">
               dalewking's answer
              </a>
              )
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               *.iml
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               local.properties
              </code>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             I think almost everyone agrees about
             <code>
              /build
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             I got sick of constantly seeing messages about the various
             <code>
              library.xml
             </code>
             files that Gradle creates or deletes in
             <code>
              /.idea
             </code>
             .  The
             <code>
              build.gradle
             </code>
             will run on the developers's local when they first check out the project, so why do those XML files need to be versioned?  Android Studio will also generate the rest of
             <code>
              /.idea
             </code>
             when a developer creates a project using
             <code>
              Check out from Version Control
             </code>
             , so why does anything in that folder need to be versioned?
            </p>
            <p>
             If the
             <code>
              *.iml
             </code>
             is versioned a new user will have to name the project exactly the same as it was when committed.  Since this is also a generated file, why version it in the first place?
            </p>
            <p>
             The
             <code>
              local.properties
             </code>
             files points to an absolute path on the file system for the SDK, so it definitely shouldn't be versioned.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Edit 1
             </strong>
             :  Added
             <code>
              .gradle
             </code>
             to ignore the gradle caching stuff that should not be versioned (thanks
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/2015129/vasily-makarov">
              Vasily Makarov
             </a>
             ).
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Edit 2
             </strong>
             :  Added
             <code>
              .DS_Store
             </code>
             now that I am using Mac.  This folder is Mac specific and should
             <strong>
              not
             </strong>
             be versioned.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Additional note
             </strong>
             : You probably also want to add a directory to put your signing keys in when building a release version.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              For copy/paste convenience
             </strong>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>.gradle
/build
/.idea
*.iml
local.properties
.DS_Store 
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

                 @mattblang yes .gitignore is auto generated when you create a new project.  It is not created however when you import a project from say Eclipse.  build/ will match all directories named "build" beneath the location of the .gitignore file.  Eg. app/build will be ignored.

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h1>
             Android Studio Arctic Fox 2020.3.1
            </h1>
            <p>
             If you create a Gradle project using Android Studio the
             <code>
              .gitignore
             </code>
             file will contain the following:
            </p>
            <h2>
             .gitignore
            </h2>
            <pre><code>*.iml
.gradle
/local.properties
/.idea/caches
/.idea/libraries
/.idea/modules.xml
/.idea/workspace.xml
/.idea/navEditor.xml
/.idea/assetWizardSettings.xml
.DS_Store
/build
/captures
.externalNativeBuild
.cxx
local.properties
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I would recommend ignoring the complete ".idea" directory because it contains user-specific configurations, nothing important for the build process.
            </p>
            <h2>
             Gradle project folder
            </h2>
            <p>
             The only thing that should be in your (Gradle) project folder after repository cloning is this structure (at least for the use cases I encountered so far):
            </p>
            <pre><code>app/
.git/
gradle/
build.gradle
.gitignore
gradle.properties
gradlew
gradlew.bat
settings.gradle
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Note: It is recommended to check-in the gradle wrapper scripts (
             <em>
              gradlew
             </em>
             ,
             <em>
              gradlew.bat
             </em>
             ) as described
             <a href="https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/gradle_wrapper.html#sec:adding_wrapper" rel="noreferrer">
              here
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              To make the Wrapper files available to other developers and execution environments you’ll need to check them into version control.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

            <p>
             I use this .gitignore. I found it at:
             <a href="http://th4t.net/android-studio-gitignore.html" rel="noreferrer">
              http://th4t.net/android-studio-gitignore.html
             </a>
            </p>
            <pre><code>*.iml
*.iws
*.ipr
.idea/
.gradle/
local.properties

*/build/

*~
*.swp
</code></pre>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="111690484" data-comment-owner-id="6501141" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-111690484">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Use just
                 <code>
                  build/
                 </code>
                 to ignore any file in any folder named build, no matter where in or nested under the folder the
                 <code>
                  .gitignore
                 </code>
                 is in. Using
                 <code>
                  /build/
                 </code>
                 will only ignore a build folder directly in the top level. Using
                 <code>
                  */build/
                 </code>
                 only looks for build folders nested 1 deep. Using
                 <code>
                  **/build/
                 </code>
                 will look recursively - I'm not sure if it starts at the top level or 1 level deep though (if at top level, then it would be same as
                 <code>
                  build/
                 </code>
                 though, so...)
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/6501141/lightcc" title="7,632 reputation">
                  LightCC
                 </a>
                </div>

        <a name="16738227">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="16738227" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="36" id="answer-16738227" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="16738227">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="36" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             36
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/16738227/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In the case of Android Studio, the only files that are required to be saved in version control are the files required to build the application from the command line using gradle. So you can ignore:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              *.iml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea
             </li>
             <li>
              build
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             However, if you save any IDE settings, such as custom code style settings, they get saved in the .idea folder. If you want those changes in version control, then you'd save the IDEA files as well (*.iml and .idea).
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2013-05-24T15:11:39" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="16738227">
               <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">
                <div class="flex--item">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="17226023" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="21" id="answer-17226023" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="17226023">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="21" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             21
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/17226023/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             My advise would be also to not ignore the .idea folder.
            </p>
            <p>
             I've imported a Git-based Eclipse project to Android Studio and that went fine. Later, I wanted to import this project with Git (like the first time) to another machine with Android Studio, but that didn't worked. Android Studio did load all the files but wasn't able to "see" the project as a project. I only could open Git-files.
            </p>
            <p>
             While importing the project for the first time (from Eclipse to Android Studio) my old .gitignore was overwritten and the new one looked like this:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              .idea/.name
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/compiler.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/copyright/profiles_settings.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/encodings.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/libraries/libs.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/misc.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/modules.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/scopes/scope_settings.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/vcs.xml
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/workspace.xml
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             So, I tried to use an empty gitignore and now it worked. The other Android Studio could load the files and the Project. I guess some files are not important
             <code>
              (profiles_settings.xml)
             </code>
             for Git and importing but I am just happy it worked.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="26290130" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="9" id="answer-26290130" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="26290130">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="9" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             9
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/26290130/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             There is NO NEED to add to the source control any of the following:
            </p>
            <pre><code>.idea/
.gradle/
*.iml
build/
local.properties
</code></pre>
            <p>
             So you can configure hgignore or gitignore accordingly.
            </p>
            <p>
             The first time a developer clones the source control can go:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Open Android Studio
             </li>
             <li>
              Import Project
             </li>
             <li>
              Browse for the build.gradle within the cloned repository and open it
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             That's all
            </p>
            <p>
             PS: Android Studio will then, through maven, get the gradle plugin assuming that your build.gradle looks similar to this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>// Top-level build file where you can add configuration options common to all sub-projects/modules.

buildscript {
    repositories {
        mavenCentral()
    }
    dependencies {
        classpath 'com.android.tools.build:gradle:0.12.2'
    }
}

allprojects {
    repositories {
        mavenCentral()
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Android studio will generate the content of .idea folder (including the workspace.xml, which shouldn't be in source control because
             <strong>
              it is generated
             </strong>
             ) and the .gradle folder.
            </p>
            <p>
             This approach is Eclipse-friendly in the way that the source control does not really know anything about Android Studio. Android Studio just needs the build.gradle to import a project and generate the rest.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="23504260" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="11" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="8" id="answer-23504260" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="23504260">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/23504260/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I support the committing of .idea  folder (excluding
             <code>
              workspace.xml
             </code>
             and
             <code>
              tasks.xml
             </code>
             ). But I am starting to come to the conclusion that .iml files should be ignored.
            </p>
            <p>
             Here is the issue:
            </p>
            <p>
             Open a project in a directory named "foo" for example and you will get foo.iml and that all seems well and good. The problem is that if I simply rename the directory to foo2 (or clone it into another directory name) when you try to open the project in Android Studio you will get three things:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              A new iml file named foo2.iml
             </li>
             <li>
              The iml file for your Android project will be changed to point now to foo2 as its parent
             </li>
             <li>
              .idea/modules.xml will have a line added for foo2.iml so it has both the old iml file and the one for the new directory
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             I can find no way to prevent Android Studio from doing this iml file generation when the project is stored in a different directory. Adding them to source control is going to cause problems. Therefore I think perhaps we should ignore *.iml files and
             <code>
              .idea/modules.xml
             </code>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                 Looking at my current project, I guess there are only 2 things I have checked in from .idea/: code style settings to enforce for the team and a user dictionary containing words specific to the project that are not real words.  I started out with many files in .idea committed, but when a file starts showing up as changed for no good reason it would get added to .gitignore.  My point was not so much that .idea should be checked in as it was to say .iml files and modules.xml should not be.
                </span>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Tested with Android Studio 3.0
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             You might need to Install
             <strong>
              .ignore
             </strong>
             plugin.
            </p>
            <p>
             You can auto-generate the .gitignore file for Android.
Right click on folder and follow
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/3NwJc.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Add .gitignore file" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/3NwJc.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Then Select Android from left panel and click
             <strong>
              Generate
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/xkBgK.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Generate .gitignore file" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/xkBgK.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Android Studio will generate .gitignore file which contains all the file need to ignore.
            </p>
            <p>
             Taken from
             <a href="http://menukanows.com/how-to-add-gitignore-file-in-android-project/" rel="noreferrer">
              http://menukanows.com/how-to-add-gitignore-file-in-android-project/
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="16832064" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="13" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="7" id="answer-16832064" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="16832064">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/16832064/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Depends on how your project format is maintained:
            </p>
            <p>
             You have two options:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Directory-based format (You will have a
              <code>
               .idea
              </code>
              folder which contains
the project specific files)
             </li>
             <li>
              File-based format (configuration files are
              <code>
               .iws
              </code>
              and
              <code>
               .ipr
              </code>
              )
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Ref:
             <a href="http://www.jetbrains.com/idea/webhelp/project.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              http://www.jetbrains.com/idea/webhelp/project.html
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Files committed to version control depends on the above:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Include .idea folder to version control, exclude
              <code>
               workspace.xml
              </code>
              and
              <code>
               tasks.xml
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              Version control
              <code>
               .ipr
              </code>
              file and all the
              <code>
               .iml
              </code>
              module files, exclude
the
              <code>
               .iws
              </code>
              file as it stores user specific settings.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Ref:
             <a href="https://intellij-support.jetbrains.com/entries/23393067" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://intellij-support.jetbrains.com/entries/23393067
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Personally I tried following advice from JetBrains but it didn't work for me. Me and another dev are using Android Studio and we had .idea and .iml file in git. I soon found out that once you start merging commits and get to all sorts of trouble when merge tool fails to merge any of the files under .idea path. As result I added all imls and .idea to gitignore. After all Studio does a very good job of creating project structure when importing Gradle project. So now I just pay close attention to what I have in my gradle files.
                </span>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="16641832">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5" itemprop="upvoteCount">

            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/16641832/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Basically any file that is automatically regenerated.
            </p>
            <p>
             A good test is to clone your repo and see if Android Studio is able to interpret and run your project immediately (generating what is missing).
             <br/>
             If not, find what is missing, and make sure it
             <em>
              isn't
             </em>
             ignored, but added to the repo.
            </p>
            <p>
             That being said, you can take example on existing
             <code>
              .gitignore
             </code>
             files, like the
             <a href="https://github.com/github/gitignore/blob/master/Android.gitignore" rel="noreferrer">
              Android one
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <pre><code># built application files
*.apk
*.ap_

# files for the dex VM
*.dex

# Java class files
*.class

# generated files
bin/
gen/

# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties

# Eclipse project files
.classpath
.project

# Proguard folder generated by Eclipse
proguard/

# Intellij project files
*.iml
*.ipr
*.iws
.idea/
</code></pre>
           </div>

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 The *.iml, *.idea and *.ipr are Android-Studio/IntelliJ specific. They are
                 <i>
                  not
                 </i>
                 needed to build the project. As they are IDE-specific, and not build-chain specific, they should probably not be checked in. Everyone can use any IDE, there is no reason to check in IntelliJ project files and not Eclipse ones, for example.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/775894/marc-plano-lesay" title="6,536 reputation">
                  Marc Plano-Lesay
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2013-10-01 06:09:54Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Oct 1, 2013 at 6:09
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 2 times">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">
                  <path d="m11.1 1.71 1.13 1.12c.2.2.2.51 0 .71L11.1 4.7 9.21 2.86l1.17-1.15c.2-.2.51-.2.71 0ZM2 10.12l6.37-6.43 1.88 1.88L3.88 12H2v-1.88Z">
                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="29848608" data-comment-owner-id="560600" data-comment-score="2" id="comment-29848608">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 2
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 If you want to work on multiple forks of the same project, or with a team where everyone uses the same IDE, or have version control of the intricate settings you use for your IDE, then yes, you should check the files in. Project files for IntelliJ are much more than simple fluff used to open your code in an editor.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/560600/sky-kelsey" title="18,990 reputation">
                  Sky Kelsey
                 </a>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="19142538">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I'm kosher with adding the .iml files and Intellij sez to add the .idea folder but ignore .idea/workspace.xml and .idea/tasks.xml, but what about .idea/libraries/ ?
            </p>
            <p>
             I don't see how it makes sense to add this.  It has a list of XML files that list libraries the Android Studio project is supposed to know about.  These are supposed to come instead from build.gradle defined dependencies -- not an IDE project file.
            </p>
            <p>
             Also the contents of one of these files looks like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;component name="libraryTable"&gt;
    &lt;CLASSES&gt;
       &lt;root url="jar://$USER_HOME$/.gradle/caches/artifacts-26/filestore/com.example/example/etc...jar!"/&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             It doesn't make sense to commit this.  What if the user specified a different home dir for gradle, or if they use a different gradle version, the path under
             <code>
              .gradle/caches/artifacts-xxx
             </code>
             is going to be different for them (i.e.
             <code>
              artifacts-
             </code>
             the number appended on the end will relate to the gradle version release you are using.)  These paths are not universal, and yet the advice is to check all this in?
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             As of Android Studio 0.8.4
             <code>
              .gitignore
             </code>
             file is generated automatically when starting new project.
By default it contains:
            </p>
            <pre><code>.gradle
/local.properties
/.idea/workspace.xml
/.idea/libraries
.DS_Store
/build
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="27387221" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="17" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="3" id="answer-27387221" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="27387221">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="3" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             3
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/27387221/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I know this is an old topic and there are certainly a lot of options, but I really prefer
             <a href="https://github.com/simonwhitaker/gibo" rel="nofollow">
              <code>
               gibo
              </code>
             </a>
             by Simon Whitaker. It's super simple to use, cross-platform (mac, *nix, and windows), and uses the github
             <a href="https://github.com/github/gitignore" rel="nofollow">
              <code>
               gitignore
              </code>
             </a>
             repo so it is (basically) always up to date.
            </p>
            <p>
             Make sure your local cache is up to date:
            </p>
            <pre><code>    $ gibo --upgrade
    From https://github.com/github/gitignore
     * branch            master     -&gt; FETCH_HEAD
    Current branch master is up to date.
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Search for the language/technology you need:
            </p>
            <pre><code>    $ gibo --search android
    Android
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Display the .gitignore file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>    $ gibo Android
    ### Android

    # Built application files
    *.apk
    *.ap_

    # Files for the Dalvik VM
    *.dex

    # Java class files
    *.class

    # Generated files
    bin/
    gen/

    # Gradle files
    .gradle/
    build/

    # Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
    local.properties

    # Proguard folder generated by Eclipse
    proguard/

    # Log Files
    *.log
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Now, append it to your project's .gitignore file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>    $ gibo Android &gt;&gt; .gitignore
</code></pre>
            <p>
             (Make sure you use
             <code>
              &gt;&gt;
             </code>
             to append to your project's .gitignore file; one
             <code>
              &gt;
             </code>
             will overwrite it - as I've done many times on accident!)
            </p>
            <p>
             I know this isn't answering the OP's exact question, but using gibo makes it so you pretty much don't have to think about 'the question' anymore! .. it's nice! ;)
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="32686466">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             To get a better idea, all you need are the following files
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              app
             </li>
             <li>
              build.gradle
             </li>
             <li>
              settings.gradle
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/l5LNa.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              <img alt="Basic Android project structure" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/l5LNa.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             You could put everything else in the .gitignore file. All your app changes lies mostly in these files and folders. The rest you see in a basic project are gradle build files or Android Studio configuration files.
            </p>
            <p>
             If you are using Android Studio, you can use "Import project" to successfully build the project. Alternatively you can build using command line, follow
             <a href="http://spring.io/guides/gs/gradle-android/" rel="nofollow noreferrer" title="Building Android Projects with Gradle">
              Building Android Projects with Gradle
             </a>
             .
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             It's best to add up the .gitignore list through the development time to prevent unknown side effect when Version Control won't work for some reason because of the pre-defined (copy/paste) list from somewhere. For one of my project, the ignore list is only of:
            </p>
            <pre><code>.gradle
.idea
libs
obj
build
*.log
</code></pre>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="42241139">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Github maintains useful gitignore items for various kinds of projects. 
Here is the list of useful gitignore items for android projects.
            </p>
            <pre><code># Built application files
*.apk
*.ap_

# Files for the ART/Dalvik VM
*.dex

# Java class files
*.class

# Generated files
bin/
gen/
out/

# Gradle files
.gradle/
build/

# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties

# Proguard folder generated by Eclipse
proguard/

# Log Files
*.log

# Android Studio Navigation editor temp files
.navigation/

# Android Studio captures folder
captures/

# Intellij
*.iml
.idea/workspace.xml
.idea/tasks.xml
.idea/gradle.xml
.idea/libraries

# Keystore files
*.jks

# External native build folder generated in Android Studio 2.2 and later
.externalNativeBuild

# Google Services (e.g. APIs or Firebase)
google-services.json

# Freeline
freeline.py
freeline/
freeline_project_description.json
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <a href="https://github.com/github/gitignore/blob/master/Android.gitignore" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              Android Gitignore in github
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="53920845" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="21" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="3" id="answer-53920845" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="53920845">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="3" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             3
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/53920845/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Using the api provided by
             <a href="https://www.gitignore.io" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              gitignore.io
             </a>
             , you can get is automatically generated. Here is the direct-link also
             <a href="https://www.gitignore.io/api/androidstudio" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              gitignore.io/api/androidstudio
             </a>
            </p>
            <pre><code>### AndroidStudio ###
# Covers files to be ignored for android development using Android Studio.

# Built application files
*.apk
*.ap_

# Files for the ART/Dalvik VM
*.dex

# Java class files
*.class

# Generated files
bin/
gen/
out/

# Gradle files
.gradle
.gradle/
build/

# Signing files
.signing/

# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties

# Proguard folder generated by Eclipse
proguard/

# Log Files
*.log

# Android Studio
/*/build/
/*/local.properties
/*/out
/*/*/build
/*/*/production
captures/
.navigation/
*.ipr
*~
*.swp

# Android Patch
gen-external-apklibs

# External native build folder generated in Android Studio 2.2 and later
.externalNativeBuild

# NDK
obj/

# IntelliJ IDEA
*.iml
*.iws
/out/

# User-specific configurations
.idea/caches/
.idea/libraries/
.idea/shelf/
.idea/workspace.xml
.idea/tasks.xml
.idea/.name
.idea/compiler.xml
.idea/copyright/profiles_settings.xml
.idea/encodings.xml
.idea/misc.xml
.idea/modules.xml
.idea/scopes/scope_settings.xml
.idea/dictionaries
.idea/vcs.xml
.idea/jsLibraryMappings.xml
.idea/datasources.xml
.idea/dataSources.ids
.idea/sqlDataSources.xml
.idea/dynamic.xml
.idea/uiDesigner.xml
.idea/assetWizardSettings.xml

# OS-specific files
.DS_Store
.DS_Store?
._*
.Spotlight-V100
.Trashes
ehthumbs.db
Thumbs.db

# Legacy Eclipse project files
.classpath
.project
.cproject
.settings/

# Mobile Tools for Java (J2ME)
.mtj.tmp/

# Package Files #
*.war
*.ear

# virtual machine crash logs (Reference: http://www.java.com/en/download/help/error_hotspot.xml)
hs_err_pid*

## Plugin-specific files:

# mpeltonen/sbt-idea plugin
.idea_modules/

# JIRA plugin
atlassian-ide-plugin.xml

# Mongo Explorer plugin
.idea/mongoSettings.xml

# Crashlytics plugin (for Android Studio and IntelliJ)
com_crashlytics_export_strings.xml
crashlytics.properties
crashlytics-build.properties
fabric.properties

### AndroidStudio Patch ###

!/gradle/wrapper/gradle-wrapper.jar

# End of https://www.gitignore.io/api/androidstudio
</code></pre>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I merge Github .gitignore files
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <a href="https://github.com/github/gitignore/blob/master/Android.gitignore" rel="nofollow">
               Android.gitignore
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://github.com/github/gitignore/blob/master/Global/JetBrains.gitignore" rel="nofollow">
               JetBrains.gitignore
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <pre><code>### Github Android.gitignore ### 

# Built application files
*.apk
*.ap_

# Files for the Dalvik VM
*.dex

# Java class files
*.class

# Generated files
bin/
gen/

# Gradle files
.gradle/
build/

# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties

# Proguard folder generated by Eclipse
proguard/

# Log Files
*.log

# Android Studio Navigation editor temp files
.navigation/

# Android Studio captures folder
captures/

### Github JetBrains.gitignore ### 

# Covers JetBrains IDEs: IntelliJ, RubyMine, PhpStorm, AppCode, PyCharm, CLion, Android Studio

*.iml

## Directory-based project format:
.idea/
# if you remove the above rule, at least ignore the following:

# User-specific stuff:
# .idea/workspace.xml
# .idea/tasks.xml
# .idea/dictionaries

# Sensitive or high-churn files:
# .idea/dataSources.ids
# .idea/dataSources.xml
# .idea/sqlDataSources.xml
# .idea/dynamic.xml
# .idea/uiDesigner.xml

# Gradle:
# .idea/gradle.xml
# .idea/libraries

# Mongo Explorer plugin:
# .idea/mongoSettings.xml

## File-based project format:
*.ipr
*.iws

## Plugin-specific files:

# IntelliJ
/out/

# mpeltonen/sbt-idea plugin
.idea_modules/

# JIRA plugin
atlassian-ide-plugin.xml

# Crashlytics plugin (for Android Studio and IntelliJ)
com_crashlytics_export_strings.xml
crashlytics.properties
crashlytics-build.properties
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Please read:
             <a href="https://intellij-support.jetbrains.com/hc/en-us/articles/206827587-How-to-manage-projects-under-Version-Control-Systems" rel="nofollow">
              JetBrains Support: How to manage projects under Version Control Systems
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             As of Android Studio 0.8.4 .gitignore file is generated automatically when starting new project. By default it contains:
            </p>
            <pre><code>.gradle
/local.properties
/.idea/workspace.xml
/.idea/libraries
.DS_Store
build/
/captures
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I agree with this statement, however I modify this file to change
/build to build/
(This will include /build and /app/build)
So I don't end up with all the files in app/build in my repository.
            </p>
            <p>
             Note also that if you import a project from Eclipse, the .gitignore won't be copied, or "automagically" created for you.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="59531163" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16736856" data-position-on-page="24" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-59531163" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="59531163">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/59531163/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Android Studio 3.5.3
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             I use this for my libraries and projects and it covers most of the files that generate by android studio and other famous tools:
            </p>
            <pre><code># Built application files
*.apk
*.ap_
*.aab

# Files for the ART/Dalvik VM
*.dex

# Generated files
bin/
gen/
out/
app/release/

# Gradle files
.gradle/
build/

# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties

# Log Files
*.log

# Android Studio Navigation editor temp files
.navigation/

# Android Studio captures folder
captures/

# IntelliJ
*.iml
.idea/workspace.xml
.idea/tasks.xml
.idea/gradle.xml
.idea/assetWizardSettings.xml
.idea/dictionaries
.idea/libraries
.idea/caches

# Keystore files
# Uncomment the following lines if you do not want to check your keystore files in.
#*.jks
#*.keystore

# External native build folder generated in Android Studio 2.2 and later
.externalNativeBuild

# Freeline
freeline.py
freeline/
freeline_project_description.json

# fastlane
fastlane/report.xml
fastlane/Preview.html
fastlane/screenshots
fastlane/test_output
fastlane/readme.md

#NDK
*.so
</code></pre>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This is created using the reference of
             <a href="http://gitignore.io/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              http://gitignore.io/
             </a>
             Where you can create the latest updated gitignore file for any project. For Android
             <a href="http://gitignore.io/api/androidstudio" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              http://gitignore.io/api/androidstudio
             </a>
             . Hope this helps. Currently I am using Android Studio 3.6.3
            </p>
            <pre><code># Created by https://www.gitignore.io/api/androidstudio
# Edit at https://www.gitignore.io/?templates=androidstudio

### AndroidStudio ###
# Covers files to be ignored for android development using Android Studio.

# Built application files
*.apk
*.ap_

# Files for the ART/Dalvik VM
*.dex

# Java class files
*.class

# Generated files
bin/
gen/
out/

# Gradle files
.gradle
.gradle/
build/

# Signing files
.signing/

# Local configuration file (sdk path, etc)
local.properties

# Proguard folder generated by Eclipse
proguard/

# Log Files
*.log

# Android Studio
/*/build/
/*/local.properties
/*/out
/*/*/build
/*/*/production
captures/
.navigation/
*.ipr
*~
*.swp

# Android Patch
gen-external-apklibs

# External native build folder generated in Android Studio 2.2 and later
.externalNativeBuild

# NDK
obj/

# IntelliJ IDEA
*.iml
*.iws
/out/

# User-specific configurations
.idea/caches/
.idea/libraries/
.idea/shelf/
.idea/workspace.xml
.idea/tasks.xml
.idea/.name
.idea/compiler.xml
.idea/copyright/profiles_settings.xml
.idea/encodings.xml
.idea/misc.xml
.idea/modules.xml
.idea/scopes/scope_settings.xml
.idea/dictionaries
.idea/vcs.xml
.idea/jsLibraryMappings.xml
.idea/datasources.xml
.idea/dataSources.ids
.idea/sqlDataSources.xml
.idea/dynamic.xml
.idea/uiDesigner.xml
.idea/assetWizardSettings.xml

# OS-specific files
.DS_Store
.DS_Store?
._*
.Spotlight-V100
.Trashes
ehthumbs.db
Thumbs.db

# Legacy Eclipse project files
.classpath
.project
.cproject
.settings/

# Mobile Tools for Java (J2ME)
.mtj.tmp/

# Package Files #
*.war
*.ear

# virtual machine crash logs (Reference: http://www.java.com/en/download/help/error_hotspot.xml)
hs_err_pid*

## Plugin-specific files:

# mpeltonen/sbt-idea plugin
.idea_modules/

# JIRA plugin
atlassian-ide-plugin.xml

# Mongo Explorer plugin
.idea/mongoSettings.xml

# Crashlytics plugin (for Android Studio and IntelliJ)
com_crashlytics_export_strings.xml
crashlytics.properties
crashlytics-build.properties
fabric.properties

### AndroidStudio Patch ###

!/gradle/wrapper/gradle-wrapper.jar

# End of https://www.gitignore.io/api/androidstudio
</code></pre>

            <pre><code>#built application files

# files for the dex VM
